
% ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- %
% ::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::: %
% ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- %

  De computer als theater, als schrijver van liefdesbrieven, 
  de computer als wereld,  als plaats voor revolutie, kunst als executable. 

  In **chmod +x art** presenteert make art Groningen kunstenaars die onze
  opvattingen, dromen en fantasieën over machines en code op hun kop
  zetten en laten zien dat programmeren een eindeloos intrigerende manier
  van creëren is. Code is een medium. Of het nou gebruikt wordt om
  instructies te formuleren voor een computer, ideeën voor een mens of
  allebei.
  
  Het schrijven ervan beïnvloedt en stuurt het creatieve proces van de
  kunstenaar. Ghost programmers mogen daarom thuis worden gelaten. Naast
  het belang van het zelf schijven van code is ook het laten zien van die
  code essentieel. Zonder source code blijft software art een goocheltruc.
  
  Doe het zelf en laat het zien!

  **make art** vindt plaats van 2 tot en met 7 maart 2010 in Groningen.

  Locaties Groningen (_zie website_):    
  **Sign**, WinschoterkadeHet Paleis}, Boterdiep 111    
  **Het Paleis**, Boterdiep 111    
  **Singelzaal**, Radesingel 6


% ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- %
% ::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::: %
% ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- %

  The computer as theatre, as writer of love letters,
  the computer as world, a place for revolution, 
  art as executable.

  **chmod +x art** presents artists that turn our ideas, 
  dreams and fantasies about machines and code up side down 
  and show programming as an infinitely intriguing way of creating. 
  Code is a medium. Whether it is used to formulate instructions 
  for a machine, ideas for people or both. 
  The writing of it influences and shapes the creative process of the artist. 

  For that reason, ghost programmers may be left at home. 
  Besides the importance of writing code yourself, 
  it is essential to show that code. Without source, 
  software art remains a magic trick. Do It Yourself and show us your sh*t!

  **make art** takes place from the 2nd til the 7th of March 2010 
  in Groningen, the Netherlands.

  Locations Groningen (_check site_):    
  **Sign**, WinschoterkadeHet Paleis}, Boterdiep 111    
  **Het Paleis**, Boterdiep 111    
  **Singelzaal**, Radesingel 6

  For the dutch temporary fork of the *make art* festival LAFKON
  wrote a *Free Software Layout* that generates posters based
  on a collection of code snippets, free/libre, autonomous, executed,
  included and attributed in footnotes. Make maps, not posters !)
  
  
  [The Edition](http://www.forkable.eu/generators/chmod+x/SELFPRINT)
  [Follow Research & Development](http://www.forkable.eu/memo/2009/wtf/)
  [Explore Development and Production Tree](http://www.forkable.eu/generators/chmod+x)

  #!/bin/bash
  cat <<":*" |
  _
  _ _ ____ _ _ _______|_|
  | |_ _| | _|____|_ | | _|_| | _____|
  |+----------------------------------------+_
  || chmod +x, Groningen(NL) 2-7 March 2010 |_|

  Make art is an international festival focused on Free/Libre/Open Source
  Software (FLOSS) and open content in digital arts. Make art offers
  performances, presentations, workshops and an exhibition, focused on the
  blurred line between art and software programming.
  
  The fifth edition - chmod +x art - will take place in Groningen (NL),
  from the 2nd to the 7th of March 2010.
  
  Workshop hello wor(l)d!, exhibition, Hocus Pocus lecture evening,
  Placard headphone concert, breakfast club, speed geeking & PechaGnucha,
  bookshop.
  
  With: Wayne Clements (GB), Martin Howse (GB), Graham Harwood (GB),
  IOhannes Zmölnig (AT), Pall Thayer (IS), Dave Griffiths (GB), Gabor
  Papp (HU), Agoston Nagy (HU), Florian Cramer (DE), Nathalie Magnan (FR),
  Dmytri Kleiner (RU), ...
  
  http://makeart.goto10.org/chmod+x
  
  -- 
  
  Make art is een internationaal festival rond Free/Libre/Open Source
  Software (FLOSS) en open content in digitale kunst. Make art biedt
  performances, presentaties, workshops en een expositie, rond de vage
  grens tussen kunst en het programmeren van software.
  
  De vijfde editie - chmod +x art - vindt plaats in Groningen (NL) van
  2 tot en met 7 maart 2010.
  
  Workshop hello wor(l)d!, expositie, Hocus Pocus lezingen avond, Placard
  koptelefoon concert, breakfast club, speed geeking & PechaGnucha,
  boekwinkel.
  
  Met: Wayne Clements (GB), Martin Howse (GB), Graham Harwood (GB),
  IOhannes Zm??lnig (AT), Pall Thayer (IS), Dave Griffiths (GB), Gabor
  Papp (HU), Agoston Nagy (HU), Florian Cramer (DE), Nathalie Magnan (FR),
  Dmytri Kleiner (RU), ...
  
  http://makeart.goto10.org/chmod+x
  
  :*
  
  sed "s|[^A-Za-z]| |g" | sed "s| *| |g" | ( cat <<"=(^-^)=" |
  #define _BSD_SOURCE
  #include <stdio.h>
  #include <stdlib.h>
  #include <time.h>
  #include <unistd.h>
  const int N=27;int main(int argc,char**argv){int count[N][N][N][N],
  i,j,k,l;for(i=0;i<N;++i){for(j=0;j<N;++j){for(k=0;k<N;++k){for(l=0;
  l<N;++l){count[i][j][k][l]=0;}}}}i=0;j=0;k=0;while(0<=(l=getchar())
  ){if('A'<=l&&l<='Z'){l-='A'-1;}else if('a'<=l&&l<='z'){l-='a'-1;}
  else{l=0;}count[i][j][k][l]++;i=j;j=k;k=l;}unsigned char probs[N][N
  ][N][N];for(i=0;i<N;++i){for(j=0;j<N;++j){for(k=0;k<N;++k){int
  total=0;for(l=0;l<N;++l){total+=count[i][j][k][l];}if(total==0){
  total=1;}int p=0;for(l=0;l<N;++l){p+=count[i][j][k][l];probs[i][j][
  k][l]=(255*p)/total;}}}}srand(time(0));i=0;j=0;k=0;while(1){
  unsigned char r=rand();int c=0;for(l=0;l<N;++l){if(probs[i][j][k][l
  ]>=r){c=l;break;}}putchar(" abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz"[c]);fflush(
  stdout);i=j;j=k;k=c;usleep(40000);}}
  =(^-^)=
  gcc -xc -std=c99 -Wall -pedantic -o chmodxart - && ./chmodxart )

  Make art is an international festival focused on Free/Libre/Open Source
  Software (FLOSS) and open content in digital arts. Make art offers
  performances, presentations, workshops and an exhibition, focused on the
  blurred line between art and software programming. =
  
  
  The fifth edition - chmod +x art - will take place in Groningen (NL),
  from the 2nd to the 7th of March 2010. =
  
  
  Workshop hello wor(l)d!, exhibition, Hocus Pocus lecture evening,
  Placard headphone concert, breakfast club, speed geeking & PechaGnucha,
  bookshop.

  IOhannes Zm=F6lnig (AT), Pall Thayer (IS), Dave Griffiths (GB), Gabor
  Papp (HU), Agoston Nagy (HU), Florian Cramer (DE), Nathalie Magnan (FR),

  http://makeart.goto10.org/chmod+x

  Make art is een internationaal festival rond Free/Libre/Open Source
  Software (FLOSS) en open content in digitale kunst. Make art biedt
  performances, presentaties, workshops en een expositie, rond de vage
  grens tussen kunst en het programmeren van software.
  
  De vijfde editie - chmod +x art - vindt plaats in Groningen (NL) van
  2 tot en met 7 maart 2010.
  
  Workshop hello wor(l)d!, expositie, Hocus Pocus lezingen avond, Placard
  koptelefoon concert, breakfast club, speed geeking & PechaGnucha,

  sed "s|[^A-Za-z]| |g" | sed "s|  *| |g" | ( cat <<"=3D(^-^)=3D" |
  #define _BSD_SOURCE
  #include <stdio.h>
  #include <stdlib.h>
  #include <time.h>
  #include <unistd.h>
  const int N=3D27;int main(int argc,char**argv){int count[N][N][N][N],
  i,j,k,l;for(i=3D0;i<N;++i){for(j=3D0;j<N;++j){for(k=3D0;k<N;++k){for(l=3D0;
  l<N;++l){count[i][j][k][l]=3D0;}}}}i=3D0;j=3D0;k=3D0;while(0<=3D(l=3Dgetcha=
  r())
  ){if('A'<=3Dl&&l<=3D'Z'){l-=3D'A'-1;}else if('a'<=3Dl&&l<=3D'z'){l-=3D'a'-1=
  ;}
  else{l=3D0;}count[i][j][k][l]++;i=3Dj;j=3Dk;k=3Dl;}unsigned char probs[N][N
  ][N][N];for(i=3D0;i<N;++i){for(j=3D0;j<N;++j){for(k=3D0;k<N;++k){int
  total=3D0;for(l=3D0;l<N;++l){total+=3Dcount[i][j][k][l];}if(total=3D=3D0){
  total=3D1;}int p=3D0;for(l=3D0;l<N;++l){p+=3Dcount[i][j][k][l];probs[i][j][
  k][l]=3D(255*p)/total;}}}}srand(time(0));i=3D0;j=3D0;k=3D0;while(1){
  unsigned char r=3Drand();int c=3D0;for(l=3D0;l<N;++l){if(probs[i][j][k][l
  ]>=3Dr){c=3Dl;break;}}putchar(" abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz"[c]);fflush(
  stdout);i=3Dj;j=3Dk;k=3Dc;usleep(40000);}}
  =3D(^-^)=3D
  gcc -xc -std=3Dc99 -Wall -pedantic -o chmodxart - && ./chmodxart )

  Hi Christoph!

  You haven't even recovered from make art Poitiers yet, and here's
  another question for you: would you (LAFKON) be interested in also
  doing the design for chmod +x art? It is a smaller edition of make
  art, taking place in Groningen (NL) produced by Sign gallery and
  curated by GOTO10.

  This is what we are looking for:
  1. a flyer
  2. a poster
  3. a small redesign of the make art website, we can use your design
  for make art 2009, and change only the color scheme plus a small tweak
  of the logo for example, to make it clearly a different edition.
  4. ecard
  5. sticker

  There is a 500.- budget for the design, but this is flexible to a
  certain extent. Are you interested in doing the design? And if so,
  what would this cost?

  Note: this event is produced by Sign and me, and we hope to have a
  much more smooth production, also when it comes to delivering (final
  versions of) texts, communication in general, etc.

  Thanks for considering :)

  Best wishes,
  Marloes

  e.g. goto10 announcements in plain ascii.

  in combination with an ascii announcement, although a simple jpg would
  be less work, is more practically.
  what do you think?

  so scheduling depends basically on the amount of work.

  Hi Marie-Jeanne and Ron, CC Christoph,

  After a little thought about the ecard, it makes more sense to us to
  do 1 emailing with ascii art + code instead of an image.

  It matches the theme of the festival much better.

  In a nutshell, it would be a simple announcement, wrapped in code that
  can be compiled and executed (see attachment of previous make art
  announce as example), and the ascii art (make art logo) can be
  pimped/redesigned by LAFKON instead of them designing an ecard.

  Let me know what you think!
  Best,
  Marloes

  dear all,

  > I've asked Sign about the exact budget and suggest you
  > remain in contact with them directly about this,
  > they are managing the budget and have contact with the printer.

  i would like to ask how printing will be handled. because posters
  are output by a generative process we did use for makeart poitiers b/w
  prints from a laser printer (instead of offset) to get unique copies.
  for the printing of unique posters there is not an out-of-the-box easy
  solution to get the printing done like e.g. flyerwire.
  so we have to decide on formats and number and see if it can be handled
  by your printer or another.

  a printing shop in essen/germany which offers following conditions:
  ----------------------------------------------------------

  -b/w plots on white paper:

     -- A0: 1,05 €
     -- A1: 0,71 €
     -- A2: 0,46 €

  b/w plots on neon paper:

     -- A0: 3,24 €
     -- A1: 2,35 €
     -- A2: 1,97 €

  b/w plots on coloured paper:

     -- A0: 3,24 €
     -- A1: 2,02 €
     -- A2: 1,34 €

  ----------------------------------------------------------
  here you can download some pictures of the testprints to get an impression:
  http://www.lafkon.net/exchange/makeartwtf_printtests.tar.gz

  please let me know asap.

  best regards,
  christoph

  dear Christoph could you make another advertisement for the Dutch
  artmagazine Tubelight? Design can be exactly the same as for Neural but then
  according Tubelight standards (see text below for conditions)
  Deadine is Saturday 23th of January and send it to lnngis@gmail.com
  Half a page 121 x 164 cm. (hxb)!! (horizontal)

  PS today you will get our answer about the posters. greetings Marie-Jeanne
  Ameln

  Conditions Tubelight (I translate it hope it is understandable otherwise see
  the Dutch text.

  Macintosh Illustrator EPS, fonts always turn to =93lettercontouren=94
  (outlines).
  QuarkXPress not lower than version 6.0 (email files  compress to  .sit or
  .zip files).
  Adobe Photoshop till  CS, foto 300dpi deliver as tiff of line art 600dpi as
  .eps.
  Adobe Indesign till CS Pdf-files which are optimize for print.
  Half a page 121 x 164 cm. (hxb)!!
  Apple Macintosh surroundings
  Deliver the digital advertisement 1:1 low resoltion pdf, plus a screenshot
  or  print

  DUTCH VERSION:
  Macintosh Illustrator EPS, fonts altijd naar lettercontouren (outlines)
  omzetten.
  QuarkXPress niet lager dan versie 6.0 (email bestanden comprimeren naar .sit
  of .zip bestanden).
  Adobe Photoshop t/m CS, foto 300dpi als .tiff aanleveren of line art 600dpi
  als .eps aanleveren.
  Adobe Indesign t/m CS Pdf-bestanden die drukgeoptimaliseerd zijn.
  Houd hiernaast genoemde afmetingen voor de opmaak van advertenties aan. Alle
  bestanden moeten geschikt zijn voor gebruik in een Apple Macintosh omgeving.
  Lever altijd gebruikte lettertypes en beeldmateriaal mee. Van de
  aangeleverde digitale advertentie dient 1:1 lage resolutie pdf, een
  screenshot of een print meegeleverd te worden.

  > dear all,

  > i would like to ask how printing will be handled. because posters
  > are output by a generative process we did use for makeart poitiers b/w
  > prints from a laser printer (instead of offset) to get unique copies.
  > for the printing of unique posters there is not an out-of-the-box easy
  > solution to get the printing done like e.g. flyerwire.
  > so we have to decide on formats and number and see if it can be handled by
  > your printer or another.
  >
  > a printing shop in essen/germany which offers following conditions:
  > ----------------------------------------------------------
  >
  > -b/w plots on white paper:
  >
  >  -- A0: 1,05 =80
  >  -- A1: 0,71 =80
  >  -- A2: 0,46 =80
  >
  > b/w plots on neon paper:
  >
  >  -- A0: 3,24 =80
  >  -- A1: 2,35 =80
  >  -- A2: 1,97 =80
  >
  > b/w plots on coloured paper:
  >
  >  -- A0: 3,24 =80

  >  -- A2: 1,34 =80

  > ----------------------------------------------------------

  >>>>>> 2010/1/12 Christoph Haag <hpotsirhc@lafkon.net>
  >>>>>>
  >>>>>>  dear all,
  >>>>>>
  >>>>>>>  I've asked Sign about the exact budget and suggest you remain in
  >>>>>>> contact
  >>>>>>>
  >>>>>>>  with them directly about this, they are managing the budget and have
  >>>>>>>> contact
  >>>>>>>> with the printer.
  >>>>>>>>
  >>>>>>>>  i would like to ask how printing will be handled. because posters
  >>>>>>>>
  >>>>>>> are output by a generative process we did use for makeart poitiers
  >>>>>>> b/w
  >>>>>>> prints from a laser printer (instead of offset) to get unique copies.
  >>>>>>> for the printing of unique posters there is not an out-of-the-box
  >>>>>>> easy
  >>>>>>> solution to get the printing done like e.g. flyerwire.
  >>>>>>> so we have to decide on formats and number and see if it can be
  >>>>>>> handled
  >>>>>>> by
  >>>>>>> your printer or another.
  >>>>>>>
  >>>>>>> a printing shop in essen/germany which offers following conditions:
  >>>>>>> ----------------------------------------------------------
  >>>>>>>
  >>>>>>> -b/w plots on white paper:
  >>>>>>>
  >>>>>>>  -- A0: 1,05 =80
  >>>>>>>  -- A1: 0,71 =80
  >>>>>>>  -- A2: 0,46 =80
  >>>>>>>
  >>>>>>> b/w plots on neon paper:
  >>>>>>>
  >>>>>>>  -- A0: 3,24 =80
  >>>>>>>  -- A1: 2,35 =80
  >>>>>>>  -- A2: 1,97 =80
  >>>>>>>
  >>>>>>> b/w plots on coloured paper:
  >>>>>>>
  >>>>>>>  -- A0: 3,24 =80
  >>>>>>>  -- A1: 2,02 =80
  >>>>>>>  -- A2: 1,34 =80
  >>>>>>>
  >>>>>>> ----------------------------------------------------------
  >>>>>>> here you can download some pictures of the testprints to get an
  >>>>>>> impression:
  >>>>>>> http://www.lafkon.net/exchange/makeartwtf_printtests.tar.gz
  >>>>>>>
